}\n\n  function flushBuckets() {\n    if (probeBucket && probeBucket.count > 0) {\n      enqueueRow(\n        makeRow(\n          probeBucket.kind,\n          \"Probe lifecycle activity\",\n          {\n            ts: probeBucket.lastTs,\n            text: `${probeBucket.count} ${probeBucket.kind} events \u00B7 run ${probeBucket.runId}`,\n          },\n          \"probe\"\n        )\n      );\n function dispatchWindowEvent(ev) {\n    try {\n      window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent(\"mb.task.event\", { detail: ev }));\n    } catch {}\n  }\n\n  function parseMaybeJSON(raw) {\n    try {\n     }\n    }\n\n    if (!ev.kind) ev.kind = eventName;\n\n    const key = `${eventName}|${ev.kind}|${ev.ts ?? \"\"}|${ev.task_id ?? \"\"}|${ev.run_id ?? \"\"}|${ev.cursor ?? \"\"}|${ev.message ?? \"task.completed\" ? \"success\" :\n      kind === \"task.failed\" ? \"error\" :\n      runId === \"policy.probe.run\" ? \"probe\" :\n      \"normal\";\n\n    enqueueRow(\n      makeRow(\n        kind,\n        kind === \"task.completed\"\n          ? \"Task completed\"\n          : kind === \"task.failed\"\n          ? \"Task failed\"\n          : \"Task event\",\n        { ts: typeof ev.ts ensurePanel();\n\n    if (es) {\n      try { es.close(); } catch {}\n      es = null;\n    }\n\n    connectionState = \"connecting\";\n    syncStatus();\n\n    es = new EventSource(SSE_URL);\n\n    es.onopen = () => {\n      attempt = 0;\n      connectionState = \"open\";\n      syncStatus();\n      enqueueRow(\n        makeRow(\n          \"sse.open\",\n          \"Stream connected\",\n try { es.close(); } catch {}\n      es = null;\n\n      flushBuckets();\n\n      attempt += 1;\n      const delay = Math.min(15000, 500 * Math.pow(2, Math.min(6, attempt)));\n\n      enqueueRow(\n        makeRow(\n          \"sse.error\",\n          \"Stream reconnecting\",\n          { ts: Date.now(), text: `Retrying in ${delay}ms` },\n          \"error\"\n        )\n      );\n\n
